Umang-2025
About KLS
More than three-quarters of a century ago, many eminent lawyers and visionaries from the North Karnataka region, who also happened to be leading lights in the Freedom Struggle, looked far ahead and decided that making legal education accessible to citizens of North Karnataka was a worthy goal, whatever the difficulty. Thus seven eminent lawyers ‚Äì N. S. Shrikhande, V.A. Naik, V. D. Belvi, B. N. Datar, S. N. Angadi. R. Kotbagi, D. S. Paramaj came together to form the Karnatak Law Society in 1939 in Belagavi. Shrimant Raja Lakhamgouda Sardesai of Vantmuri trusted these Founder Members to be true to their vision and a Promissory Note totaling Rs. 1 Lakh was executed by him to support the application for opening a new Law College. Many of these founder members, and other legal scholars from this region volunteered to teach at this College despite lucrative practice, and extensive personal and social commitments.
Belagavi thus became a renowned education centre for Law education. Students from Andhra Pradesh, Kerala and Maharashtra took admission and proved to be active in social, political and judicial fields. The first batch of Raja Lakhamgouda College started operating in 1939, graduated in 1941. Since then, more than 7500 students have passed through the hallowed portals of this esteemed institution. A few notables among the many luminaries that this college has produced include ‚Äì Shri. E. S. Venkataramiah, Former Chief Justice of India, Shri. S. Rajendra Babu, Former Chief Justice of India & Chairman, National Human Rights Commission, .and Shri. K. K. Venugopal, Present Attorney General of India.
Today, Karnatak Law Society (KLS) has the distinction of running schools, and colleges in the fields of Law, Commerce, Engineering and Management Education and all its Institutions have earned reputation of being as leading institutions in Karnataka.

Our history
2004
Karnatak Law Society having established a number of institutions in the city of Belagavi which have identity as Quality Educational Institutions started ‚ÄúVishwanathrao Deshpande Institute of Technology‚Äù(VDIT) at Haliyal in 2004-05 by the initiation and support of Shri R V Deshpande former minister Government of Karnataka.
Within a short span of years, VDIT has developed excellent infrastructural facilities and an academic climate to train the students to meet the challenges posed by rapid changing techno-economic scenario. The institution has an excellent, well qualified and experienced faculty. The Institute is located on a 26 acres campus, cradled by a picturesque landscape.

Principal Message
Message:
Established in 2004, with intention of imparting quality engineering education, our institute has been a hub of many activities of excellence and achievements both by students and staff. We are committed to provide better academic ambience and strive for multifaceted development of students. The website would provide an effective platform to showcase all such details.
We are sure that, VDIT will reach newer heights in the days to come with cooperation from all stakeholders.
I wish the students a comfortable stay in the campus and colorful future.

Umang-2025
Admission
Admissions for the academic year-2025-26 under Management quota can contact Prof.Gururaj Joshi - Mobile No-9448420102 and Dr. Vinod Naik - Mobile No - 8884324070
ELIGIBILITY FOR SEEKING ADMISSION TO THE B.E. 1ST SEMESTER THROUGH CET AND MANAGEMENT QUOTA
Must have passed 12th class exam or second year pre university or equivalent
Must have compulsory subjects along with Chemistry/Bio-Technology/Biology/Electronics/Computer Science as optional subjects with English as one of the languages of study
An aggregate minimum of 45% Physics and Mathematics along with Chemistry / Bio-technology / Biology / Electronics / Computer marks for general category (40% for SC, ST, Cat-1, 2A, 2B, 3A and 3B category candidates) and 40% for in optional subjects in qualifying examination is required.
THE MINIMUM QUALIFICATION FOR SEEKING ADMISSION TO THE B.E. HAVING DIPLOMA IN ANY ENGINEERING DISCIPLINE
Candidate must have minimum aggregate marks 45% of V & VI semester (40% marks in case of SC/ST & OBC).
The candidates having Diploma from Karnataka and coming through CET cell are eligible for admission to 3
rd
semester B.E in the branch of their study in Diploma.
A candidate who is admitted to the 3
rd
semester will have to study bridge courses as prescribed in the syllabus supplied by VTU.
DOCUMENTS REQUIRED FOR ADMISSION UNDER MANAGEMENT QUOTA
SSLC / X Marks Card
PUC-II / XII Marks Card
Study Certificate for 7 years ( 5 years from high school & 2 years from college)
Character Certificate
Annual Income Certificate (In case of Category) (Not Applicable for Non-Karnataka Students)

NIRF
ABOUT NIRF ( NATIONAL INSTITUTE RANKING FRAMEWORK )
The National Institutional Ranking Framework (NIRF) was approved by the MHRD and launched by Honorable Minister of Human Resource Development on 29th September 2015.
This framework outlines a methodology to rank institutions across the country. The methodology draws from the overall recommendations broad understanding arrived at by a Core Committee set up by MHRD, to identify the broad parameters for ranking various universities and institutions. The parameters broadly cover ‚ÄúTeaching, Learning and Resources,‚Äù ‚ÄúResearch and Professional Practices,‚Äù ‚ÄúGraduation Outcomes,‚Äù ‚ÄúOutreach and Inclusivity,‚Äù and ‚ÄúPerception‚Äù.
The Data Submitted for India Rankings-2025 of our college is as follows:
Innovation
Engineering

Anti-Ragging Committee
As per the notification of AICTE dated 01.07.2009, ragging is totally banned in the campus and any one found guilty of ragging is liable to be punished.
PUNISHMENTS:
Cancellation of admission.
Suspension from attending classes.
Suspension / Expulsion from the Hostel.
Rustication from the Institution for period of ragging from 1-4 semesters.
Expulsion from the Institution and consequent debarring from admission to any other institution.
Anti Ragging Circulars / Notices from UGC, New Delhi
Click Here

Internal Complaints Committee

Punishment:
Penalties
range from one to three years imprisonment and/or a fine. Additionally, with
sexual harassment
being a crime, employers are obligated to report offences.

Anti- Sexual Harassment Squad
ACTIVITIES OF THE SQUAD.
Visiting college campus, hostel, classrooms, college bus frequently.
Further, would find out any harassment activities if at all happened in the college campus or any college related places.
They also educate the students about harassment and its ill effects as well as legal complications if involved in the harassment.
If they find any harassment, they will initiate necessary legal actions on the person.
They also periodically, collect feedback from the students about harassment.

ECO CLUB
Objective
Eco Club aims of making the students aware of environmental issues and their duties towards the nature.
It focuses on generating interest about resource conservation, create¬†awareness¬†of biodiversity conservation, sustainable development and other environmental issues among the student community.
It aims to create a clean and¬†green¬†consciousness among students through various activities.

Campus Code of Conduct
Keep the campus neat and clean. Do not put any waste anywhere in the campus except in the waste baskets provided at every corner
KLS VDIT has received certificate of Appreciation for their significant contribution in one student one tree initiative of ALL INDIA COUNCIL FOR TECHNICAL EDUCATION on 3rd December 2019. It‚Äôs the Earnest request to everyone to plant more tress and join your hands in maintaining the greenery and do not damage the pots or life of a plant.
Did you know that although 70 percent of planet Earth is covered with water, only 1% of it is available for human consumption? Every drop of water counts. Save water to save ourselves. Reduce the personal water demand. Turn off the Tap when not in use.
Do not eat in places where it is advisable not to do so.
Join your hands to make the campus Plastic free zone. Plastic water bottle, Plastics carry bags are banned instead use any eco friendly material like glass, ceramic, stainless steel or any biodegradable material.
No smoking in the Campus
Do not post posters without approval.
The application of ethical codes is not confined to internal use at the institution. Students are representatives of their college outside of the campus as well and must therefore behave in the same way.
Events
On the occasion of Ganesh Chaturthi Eco Club VDIT has come up with awareness video on use of Eco Friendly materials for Ganesh idols and hazardous effect on use of POP and the toxicity of heavy metals in the colors used to paint idols. Follow the Covid-19 protocols and Be safe.
ECO CLUB of KLS Vishwanathrao Deshpande Institute of Technology, Haliyal organized webinar on Water Conservation Techniques on 15th May 2021 Under Jal Shakti Abhiyan
We at KLS VDIT, are determined to change ourselves by undertaking actions before telling others to act and have taken the Pledge for Carbon Neutral Campus under AICTE SCCN(Smart Campus Cloud Network).
Applied for National Water award ‚Äì Best Institution for campus usage- Government of India- Ministry of jai Shakti.
Applied for AICTE Green Campus Award.
Institution IGBC ‚Äì Indian Green Building Council membership.
Eco club LOGO design competition from VDIT students on 22-9-2020.
Tree Plantation Event for students of KLS VDIT, to plant at least one sample in their locality in view of National Service Scheme Day on 24th Sept 2020.
To protect our depleting OZONE LAYER awareness activity was organized on World Ozone day, 16th Sep, 2020. All the faculty have taken the pledge to pant more tress and to save water.
In an earnest attempt to lend a green touch to the Institution‚Äôs environment and sensitize the students about their role in conserving it, KLS‚ÄôS Vishwanathrao Deshpande Institute of Technology along with NSS unit VTU Belagavi, in co-ordination with NSS unit KLS‚Äôs VDIT Haliyal conducted Van Mahotsava on 13th July 2019 in the campus. The celebration was and ideal opportunity to install the value of social responsibility in the students towards safeguarding trees and forests and to conserve water. We have also received certificate of Appreciation for their significant contribution in one student one tree initiative of AICTE on 3rd December 2019.
Department of Civil Engg has conducted clean campus drive and collected plastic as part of ‚ÄúSwatchtha Hi Seva‚Äù campaign as per the direction of AICTE. The campaign started on 20/09/2019 by taking a pledge of plastic free campus. All the faculty members and students joined their hands in collecting plastic near Civil Engg. Block, KLS VDIT.
Every point of water utilization is with a signboard ‚ÄúTo save water and to Maintain Cleanliness in the campus and also Eco Club VDIT has displayed its objective and rules every corner in the campus.
Save water drive was organized at KLS VDIT campus on March 23, 2019. All the faculty and students have taken a pledge to save water and to plant the samplings to maintain greenery all around.
KLS VDIT Students had presented a skit at Highlighted place of Haliyal to give awareness to public to Save water and conserve tress on August 16, 2018
As a awareness activities to students ‚ÄúModel making event was organized on April 22, 2018. In this event Rainwater harvesting structures were prepared and exhibited by students and gave an awareness to conserve water.

NSS
The NSS‚Äôs motto, ‚ÄúNot Me But You,‚Äù captures the spirit of democratic behaviour and upholds the necessity of selfless service. The NSS fosters in students a growth in understanding other people‚Äôs perspectives and a respect for other living things. The NSS‚Äôs guiding concept is encapsulated in this phrase, which emphasises the idea that each person‚Äôs well-being ultimately depends on the welfare of society as a whole. As a result, NSS volunteers are expected to work towards the advancement of society.

Standards Club
About Standards Club
:
Standards Club in association with Bureau of Indian Standards (BIS), Government of India, Hubballi branch is inaugurated in KLS VDIT Haliyal by the chief guest Mr. Virendra Kadam, CEO and Founder, DELTSYS E-FORMING, Belagavi on 24/8/2023.
The Bureau of Indian Standards (BIS) is the National Standards body of India. It operates under the Ministry of Consumer Affairs, Food & Public Distribution, Government of India. BIS is responsible for the formulation, publication, and implementation of standards for various products, services, and systems to ensure their quality, safety, and reliability.
Here are some key points about BIS:
Quality consciousness, based on standardization, is one of the pillars of accelerated economic development, and priming students to appreciate the significance of quality, standards, and standardization can serve as a catalyst to improve societal awareness on these subjects.
BIS has taken the initiative of creating Standards Clubs in educational institutions comprising teachers and students as members. Through a variety of activities under these Clubs, young talents get learning opportunities in the field of quality and standardization.
Students are introduced to the concepts of Quality and Standardization with activities like Standards Writing, Quiz Competitions, Essay Writing, Poster Making, etc. in these clubs.
Standards Club members are also provided with an opportunity to visit industries and laboratories for practical understanding, complementing the theoretical study as part of the curriculum. This allows the students to appreciate the application of science concepts and understand their importance.
Benefits of BIS:
Consumer Protection:
BIS standards and certifications provide consumers with confidence that the products they purchase meet specific quality and safety standards.
Industrial Growth:
Standardization helps industries produce consistent and high-quality products, which can improve their competitiveness in domestic and international markets.
Safety:
BIS standards often focus on safety aspects, ensuring that products and services are designed and manufactured with safety in mind.
Trade Facilitation:
BIS standards align with international standards in many cases, facilitating trade and commerce by ensuring compatibility with global markets.
Quality Improvement:
BIS plays a role in promoting quality improvement across various sectors by setting benchmarks that companies strive to meet or exceed.
Environmental Impact:
BIS standards can also include guidelines for environmental sustainability, contributing to responsible and eco-friendly practices.

Umang-2025
K-Tech NAIN Center
About ‚Äì NAIN
Creation of an ecosystem that promotes innovation in educational institutions is one of the key objectives of the Startup Policy-2015. With this focus, the scheme of ‚ÄòNew Age Incubation Network‚Äô is initiated by Govt. of Karnataka, ICT Society, Bengaluru under the Department of IT, BT and S&T. This is now operational in all Districts of the state selected under 1,2 and 3 Phases.
In Third phase of New Age Incubation Network (NAIN) programme the Department of IT, BT and S&T Govt. of Karnataka selected our Institution as a NAIN Centre in the Year 2019-20.
In NAIN programme the incubators will be networked and connected to the common portal to facilitate exchange of thoughts, ideas and collaboration across institutions and disciplines.
Under the NAIN, Students are encouraged to identify local problems and address those using concepts of frugal innovation, and to develop appropriate technology based solutions and working prototypes. And also mentors assigned to the students help them to formulate a business model based on the new technology and encourage them to think like entrepreneurs.
Financial assistance for running the NAIN incubators and for student projects initially provided for three years from 2019-20 to 2021-22 and further extended for two more years from 2022-23.
Government provide Operational support from date of selection in the form of grant support. The grant will be provided to the Host Institute for the NAIN facility under the following two heads:
(i) NAIN ‚Äì Operational Expenses (N-OPX) and
(ii) NAIN ‚Äì Student Project Seed Fund (N-SPF)
NAIN Operational Expenses Grant of Rs. 10 lakh per annum, for salary of one Full-time employee, funds for organizing events like Ideathons, Hackathons, Entrepreneurship boot camps etc. meeting, Travel and other miscellaneous expenses. Contingent & Administrative overheads.
NAIN Student Project Seed Fund Grant: A seed fund of up to Rs. 3 lakh per project shall be awarded to every selected team. Up to 10 teams shall be funded in each Host Institute (total fund granted to NHI = Rs. 30 lakh per annum). This fund shall be released to student innovators.
In Project Batch-I, totally 10 local problems identified by our students in the field of Agriculture, Solar distillation, CCTV Camera security, and safety driving system total worth of Rs. 13.8 lakh Rupees.
Objectives of K-Tech NAIN Center
The main objective is to encourage students, research scholars and alumni to share their ideas to solve chosen problems which are local centric and to validate, Refine and Nurture ideas.
Incubation center shall provide an ecosystem to convert ideas into proofs of concept and upgrade them to a level of commercial value.
After successful incubation, encourage and lead the teams towards setting up a business enterprise.
Support Provided @ K-TECH NAIN
KLS VDIT, Haliyal thrives to bridge the gap between theoretical and practical learning and the centers like JAGRUTI- a tech Hub, Toyota -Centre of excellence, e-Yantra Lab, Welding Research Center, Thermal Engg. Research lab, along with NAIN scheme prove to be a befitting example of the same.
Technology domain areas at ‚ÄúK-tech NAIN CENTER‚Äù
Cooling of Electronic devices.
Design and Welding of Aerospace material.
Analysis, Design and Fabrication of Robotic and Automation systems.
IOT in Agricultural field.
Mini Project Exhibition:
To imbibe in the young minds the idea of innovation, an annual mini project exhibition is organized for the first year students.
Panel Discussions:
Students are encouraged to have panel discussion over on -going real time projects with eminent personalities in the relevant field as panelists.
Technical Talks:
In order to educate the students regarding the expectations from the industry, technical talks from industry experts is a tradition followed at KLS, VDIT.
Empanelment: KLS VDIT has empanelment with leading organizations which gives an insight to the students with regards to be industry -ready.
Ideathon:
Organized at college, ‚Äú Ideathon‚Äù invites problem statement and solution for the same in marketable format from the students and alumni .The best ideas are then chosen for NAIN.
YEP:
To inform the students from Government schools and Pre -University College regarding how their ideas can be turned into prototypes and inform them regarding the support provided by NAIN, ‚ÄúYoung Entrepreneurs Program‚Äù is organized.
BOOT CAMP:
To give an insight to participants as to how ideas =formulation can be made and to have one-on-one discussion with mentors and entrepreneurs, ‚ÄúBOOT CAMP ‚Äúis organized.
Through these initiatives top 20 ideas/proposals will be selected for the new age incubation network to submit the final proposals.
Path to Turn Idea to Product
Under NAIN , the workshops like YEP and Boot camps are organized to identify potential ideas.
The selected ideas are turned into project proposals by the guidance of mentors ( academicians/ local entrepreneurs ) who guide the students with regards to financial aspects. The proposals then undergo a scrutiny by the expert team comprising of academicians, industrialists and local entrepreneurs.
The selected proposals are then sent to KITS for the funding approval.
NAIN centre at college provides facilities like infrastructure, space, internet, mentor support, guidance for intellectual property rights (patent filing) and start-up formation I.e., company formation.
Activities
Developing an entrepreneurship mind-set amongst students through specially crafted Young¬†¬† Entrepreneur Program, for students to understand the basics of entrepreneurship from experienced entrepreneurs and start-ups.
Identify regional and local problems by conduction of Hackthon or inviting ideas and creating statement of problems.
Sharing of statement of problems among students, Research scholars, and Alumni.
Getting ideas, solutions from students, Research scholars, and Alumni through work shop,
Seminar and Webinars
.
Formation of team refining of ideas and solutions and convert them to project proposal along with costing and other details.
Placing proposal before the screening committee for sanctioning of fund.
Reviewing of project process quarterly by screening committee.
Institution-Level Innovation Council (IIC), This committee meet once in a quarter and initiate all steps for promoting innovation in education for developing an ecosystem where students are given the necessary resources and support to convert their ideas into proof of concept and create IPs.

IIT-B, Spoken Tutorial
Letter Of Association with Indian Institute of Technology¬† Bombay. Academic year May 2022-23.
Click Here
Karnatak Law Society‚Äôs,Vishwanathrao Deshpande Institute of Technology (KLS VDIT) is running IIT Bombay Spoken Tutorial E-Tutor Training program (Resource Center) since 2016
. It is a project of NME-ICT, recognized by MHRD and Govt. of India, and developed at IIT Bombay. The Spoken Tutorial Project is about teaching and learning a particular FOSS (Free and Open Source Software) like Linux, Scilab, LaTeX, PHP & MySQL, Java, C/C++, LibreOffice etc. via an easy Video tool ‚Äì Spoken Tutorials. Today, SMEs and Govt. departments are moving to Open Source Software like Linux OS. Students with this knowledge will have an edge in the job market. They can also become entrepreneurs and use Open Source Software in their businesses, and save money vs., if they were using commercial software. Net ‚Äì it is a win-win situation for all.
Benefits:
Training Programs run on Self Learning Mode or Remote Learning, no expert is required to teach the students. Faculty coordinators from various departments enroll students & students download online tutorials & generate test request.
IIT Bombay Spoken Tutorials E-Tutor Training programs are mapped with B.E course syllabus for teaching.
Spoken Tutorial acts as e-Resource for students to understand the technical concepts along with providing students with certification from IIT Bombay for appearing and clearing the test.
Students learn all available courses through Spoken Tutorial in the lab hours and also in their free time while online Test is conducted in college campus.
IIT Bombay Spoken Tutorials E-Tutor Training programs help students for their career with recruiters and at PG interviews.
For More info.: https://spoken-tutorial.org/

JAGRUTI

The Tech Hub
JAGRUTI, is the abode for innovative and advanced technological gears those ignite the curiosity in the minds of students. The venue consists various technological ideas and implements contributed by many renowned industries and students of the Institute. These collections cover all branches of Engineering like Mechanical Engineering, Civil Engineering, Electrical & Electronics Engineering, Electronics & Communication Engineering, Computer Science & Engineering.
The Tech Hub consists the various Equipment/Components from different Contributors.

Adequacy of JAGRUTI Tech Hub
Mechanical Engineering
1.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Volvo engine and transmission model is useful in students understanding of IC engine cycles, Transmission mechanism and Propeller shaft working along with differential mechanism.
2.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Students can visualize the valve mechanisms that help them in their comprehension in hydraulics and fluid mechanics.
3.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The various composite materials used in modern products are exhibited in the venue that makes students to know about present industrial arena.
4.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The cutting tools kept in the venue make students familiar with new ways of machining.
5.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The model of 3D printer makes students to comprehend the latest modes of manufacturing.
6.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The Inspection gauges assist student understanding regarding the quality control section of any industry.
Electronics & Communication Engineering
1.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The ‚ÄúJagruti Center‚Äù it‚Äôs a technical Hub. The hub showcases all the necessary prototypes which are helpful to gain the basic idea about technologies.
2.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The Jagruti Center‚Äù in our college basically has various Electronics Boards especially FPGA, CPLD kits voltage regulator etc. As we all know Industry 4.0 leverages connectivity and autonomous operation to create robust industrial IoT applications.
3.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† The FPGA, SoC FPGA and CPLD industrial automation solutions enable industrial system designers to reduce costs and time to market significantly for factory automation system designs.
4.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Also we have the Smart water meter it‚Äôs a GPS enabled device which will give you the information about water Consumption with billing details in our mobile handset this product is manufactured by ‚ÄúDigineeru‚Äù Company Bangalore.
5.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Center allowing students to delve deeper into specific topics of interest. The center serves as a valuable resource for academic projects and research endeavors, enabling students to explore advanced concepts and theories in their chosen fields.
6.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Apart from the technical resources, the center provides mentorship and guidance to students, connecting them with industry professionals and alumni who can offer career advice and industry insights. This support system helps students in making informed decisions about their future and assists them in their professional development journey.
Computer Science & Engineering
1.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Netwroking Technologies: The technology which is used to exchange the data between small and large information.
This technology can be used in educational institutions as well as businesses
2.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Printers : A printer is an output device whose job is to print a soft file into the computer. a printer is a machine that prints any soft copy from the computer in the form of a hard copy.
3.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Communcation Technlogies: Communication technology is any digital tool you can use to send and receive information. This technology can include software, computer programs, devices and messaging systems
4.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Scanner: A document scanner is a device that can digitally copy physical objects and upload their images to computers.
5.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Computer Components: Keyboar,mouse,monitor,printer
6.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† MS Operating System: It allows users to view and store files, run the software, play games, watch videos, and provides a way to connect to the internet.
7.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Android Software: Android allows us to develop our applications and publish them on Google Play.
It comes with an application programming interface (API) for a full-featured application
8.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Artificial Intelligence(Application): AI is used in robotics, defense, transport, healthcare, marketing, business, gaming, banking
9.¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† ChatGPT(Application): It is an AI-based bot developed by an Artificial Intelligence research company.
Applications:
1) Code-Writer

4)Explaining Difficult Concepts
Electrical & Electronics Engineering
1.¬†¬† Overhead transmission line insulators gives idea about how porcelin and polymer material use as insulator.
2.¬†¬†¬† Fuse, MCB, MCCB give brief idea about overcurrent protection mechanism.
3.¬†¬†¬† Pipe and plate earthing model gives information about electrical earthing.
4.¬†¬†¬† Logic gate module briefs functioning of different types of logic gates.
5.¬†¬†¬† Motor cut section gives idea of constructional aspect of machines.
6.¬†¬†¬† Underground cable model helps to know the selection of cables for different current ratings.
Civil Engineering
1.¬† Flexible pavement model: Briefs about different layers in it.
2.¬† Geological Minerals/Rocks: Gives the Importance of different minerals and rocks used in construction.
3.¬† HYSD bars: Different size bars used in construction and its importance
4.¬† Steel sections: Gives an idea about various sections used in mega constructions.
5.¬† Rain Water Harvesting: Gives an idea about the importance of rain water in day to day life
6.¬† Advanced construction block: Briefs about the importance of it with respect to technical aspects.
7.¬† Magnetic compass: To know the Magnetic north direction using magnetic bearings.
8.¬† Residential building: Gives an idea about cross section of the building.

NPTEL L C
NPTEL LOCAL CHAPTER @ KLS VDIT, Haliyal, KA, IN.
About SWAYAM-NPTEL
NPTEL (National Programme on Technology Enhanced Learning) is a joint initiative of IITs and IISc. It has been offering self-study courses across engineering, humanities and science streams for more than a decade. These are available at:
https://nptel.ac.in
. From March 2014 NPTEL has been offering online certification for its courses, the highlight being the certification exam through which the student gets an opportunity to earn a certificate form the IITs. These are available at:
https://swayam.gov.in/NPTEL
.
NPTEL Local Chapter
To take this initiative forward and to encourage more students of KLS VDIT to participate in this initiative, college has set NPTEL Local Chapter in the college under the NPTEL Nodal center at IIT Madras. This local chapter is led by a faculty member of the college, who is single Point of Contact (SPOC) to NPTEL center at IIT Madras. KLS VDIT, being a ‚ÄòLocal Chapter of NPTEL‚Äô appeal you to take the benefits of this initiative and enjoy the E-Learning, where you can study as per your mood and play/pause/forward/backward/stop your teacher as per your grasping limit. The aim of this local chapter is to uplift the knowledge/ expertise level of students and faculty members to national/ international level.
SPOC- NPTEL Local Chapter, KLS VDIT
Dr.Gururaj Hatti
Assistant Professor,
Department Of Mechanical Engineering
KLS VDIT, Haliyal-581329, KA, IN.

nptel@klsvdit.edu.in

Rooftop Solar PV System
200 kW Grid Connected Rooftop Solar PV System
A grid connected Photovoltaic (PV) system is an electricity generating solar PV power plant that is connected to utility grid. By having a grid connected system, the consumer can export the excess generated power to the utility grid.
KLS VDIT has a solar power plant of 200 kWp capacity installed at the rooftop of Main Building (150 kW) and Mechanical Building (50 kW). This plant was set up in the year 2018 by M/S. Sterling & Wilson Pvt Ltd, Bengaluru with the investment of Rs. 82 Lakh. There are totally 626 solar PV panels of 320 Wp capacity wide spread in 1,215 square meter rooftop area. It consists of 04 nos. of grid tied inverters of 50 kVA capacity. Few other important equipment of the power plant are;
Net Meter for recording both import and export of energy
SCADA (Supervisory Control and Data Acquisition) System
Earthing Provided
Lightning Arresters Provided
HT Metering Cubical
Data access using Solar
‚ÄúInvendis Solar‚Äù is a web application for accessing the system data (Data Logger)
‚Äúi~Solar‚Äù by Invendis is an android application for accessing the system data.
The daily average power generation is
616
units and monthly average is
18,500
units considering the data of year 2022. The cleaning of solar panels is carried out once in a week.

About Library
Vision
‚Ä¢To provide a student friendly learning environment that facilitates
dissemination of knowledge using modern tools.
Mission
‚Ä¢To provide comprehensive resources and services to support
research, teaching and learning needs of the user community.
‚Ä¢To augment and maintain collections in the support of the academic pursuits of the college.
‚ÄúEducation is not the amount of information that is put into your brain and runs not there, undigested, all your life. We must have life-building, man-making, character-building, assimilating fine ideas and making them your life and character, you have more education than any man who has got by heart a whole library‚Äù.
‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.. Swami Vivekananda
As Swami Vivekananda said the Library is temple of knowledge it is store house of information, where the user can get desired information. VDIT Library & Information Center is located in spacious building with area of 655sqm.

DELNET

Welding Research Center
The Karnataka Council for Technical Upgradation (KCTU) is a Joint Venture of Government of India and Government of Karnataka A Premier Council for Implementation of Schemes under Karnataka new Industrial policy 2014-19. It supports the new and existing R & D centers (public / private) to boost sustainable growth of manufacturing sector by way of partial investment in new / additional infrastructural facility including capital goods viz. 3 D printing facilities etc. The strengthening of R & D center shall facilitate innovative ideas, technology, and products to boost the manufacturing sector.
Seventh Level Committee of Karnataka Council for Technological Upgradation (KCTU) Government of Karnataka, sanctioned financial assistance of Rs. 22.78 lakhs for setting up of ‚ÄúWelding Research Center‚Äù in Mechanical Engineering Department of KLS VDRIT. The total project cost is Rs.45.55 lakhs.
"Welding Research Center‚Äù Supported By:

Purpose¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†Under Financial Assistance to R&D Center for setting up of ‚ÄúWelding Research Center‚Äù

Computer Center
About
Computer Center (CC) the neural system of VDIT provides 24√ó7 and 365 days a year uninterrupted computing and network infrastructure along with Internet, Email, Web, DNS, CCTV, FeedBack, Antivirus, to all the stakeholders of the institute. CC also provides various advanced and special purpose software like Sophos for all the campus internet users.
The center was established with the objective of providing computational environment for the academic and research community of the institute. The Center offers training and consultancy apart from being a support service for the Office, faculty, students and staff.

Facilities
After identifying core requirements in computing infrastructure and engineering discipline-specific laboratory prerequisites, the institute has established different computer laboratories. There are totally 12 well-equipped Air-conditioned labs, according to expertise areas which supports the following applications.
Linux Applications.
Windows Applications.
Programming and Applications with Online Computer Based
Training Facility
CAD/M Applications.
VLSI and Design Applications.
Network Applications.
Database Applications.
Business Applications.
VDIT‚Äôs 27+ acre lush green campus has a robust network of 500+ nodes on a fiber optic backbone and extends LAN connectivity to every corner of the campus. The campus network infrastructure, Sophos performs the mammoth task of supporting 2500+ users including students, faculty members, and other supporting staff.
Services
Institute has state of the art Central Computing Center.
The center acts as one stop solution for each and every IT need of institution.
The Center extends all support for computing services. Hardware & Software high end with required licensed software and allied equipment make it a resourceful node of service.
10 State of art laboratories with more than 500 systems.
Server room with cyberoam fire wall to provide protection from external threats of internet.
WiFi access at key locations to enable ease of exchange of information.
500Mbps OFC Leased Line high speed internet facility.
24*7 100 Mbps Internet facility.
WiFi internet facility at hostels after academic hours.
Microsoft Academic alliance for the entire campus.
24/7 surveillance at key locations at campus as well as in college buses of institution.

Hostel
One of the major concerns of parents about their wards is the facilities of stay and food. VDIT promises parental care to boys and girl students residing in the hostel.
The boys hostel accommodates 330 students and girls hostel accommodates 275 students.

Facilities
Mess ensures quality food and water purifier is installed for drinking water.
Hot water through solar system is provided at every floor. Uninterrupted power supply is provided with the help of generators.
Dispensary in the campus takes care of preliminary medical treatment.
24*7 Internet Wifi Facility for the Hostels.
Pure Drinking Water Facility has been provided in the campus using RO+UV Filtering unit.
Timings
Girls Hostel:
Opens at 6: 00 AM and Closes by 6:30PM
Boy‚Äôs Hostel:
Opens at 6:00 AM and Closes by 9:00PM
Rules and Regulations
Students are asked to be inside the hostel within the specified¬† timings. If not followed actions will be taken.
Students are asked to keep hostel and their rooms clean.
Outsiders are not allowed until permission is taken by the respective Wardens of the hostels(Boys/ Girls).
Students going home from hostel must be permitted by the hostel warden.

Scholarships
The college is supporting the students to get the scholarship from different organization. It helps poor students, economically backward and meritorious students.
Various scholarships avenues are available in the college offered by various Govt. bodies & private Organisations. The Various scholarships avenues are available in the college, offered by various Govt. bodies & private organizations. The announcement of these will be made in advance in the notice boards. It is solely responsibility of the students to seek the applications and apply. College will not be responsible for the delay in submission of application.
Types of Scholarship
SC/ST Scholarship (Social Welfare)
Ex-Service man Scholarship
DTE Scholarship
Taluk Panchayat Scholarship
Merit cum Means Scholarship
Nijalingappa Scholarship
Jindal scholarship
Sainik Kalyana Scholarship
Kittur Rani Channamma Scholarship
Post-Merit Scholarship
GSB Scholarship
Details of Scholarship Schemes
Ministry of Human Resource Development (Department of Higher Education) Govt. of India awards scholarships to candidates for those who have secured minimum 80% of marks in Class XII or equivalent examination and whose parents annual income is below or equal to Rs. 4.5 lakhs. For details visit Website:
pue.kar.nic.in
Govt. of India ‚Äì Post Matric Scholarships for Scheduled Castes / Scheduled Tribes Students.
The Post Matric Scholarships enables a considerable number of Scheduled Castes/Scheduled Tribes students to obtain post-matric and higher level of education resulting in their overall educational and economic development.
For online application filling visit Commissionarate of Social Welfare Website:
www.sw.kar.nic.in
Link: SC : POST-MATRIC SCHOLARSHIP
ST : POST-MATRIC SCHOLARSHIP
Post Matric Scholarships / Fee Concession for Backward Class Students
Online Post Matric scholarships disbursements through ePass application is one of the important welfare measures of the Government of Karnataka which is aimed at educational upliftment of students, initiated by the Department of Backward Classes Welfare.
For online application filling visit Department of Backward Classes Welfare Website:
www.karepass.cgg.gov.in
Post Matric Scholarship for Minorities (Muslims, Christians, Sikhs, Buddhists, Parsis)
For online application filling visit Directorate of Minorities Website:
www.gokdom.kar.nic.in
Ministry of Minority Affairs ‚Äì Government of India Merit-cum-Means Scholarship
Scheme For online application filling visit Minority Welfare Scholarship System Website:
www.momascholarship.gov.in.
For Guidelines on ‚ÄúHow to Apply?‚Äù Procedure and for more details, visit Directorate of Minorities Website:
www.gokdom.kar.nic.in
Govt. of India Scholarships
For students with disabilities (Physically Handicapped) For online application filling visit National Handicapped Finance and Development Corporation (NHFDC) Website:
nhfdc.nic.in
Karnataka State Wakf Foundation for Women Development ‚Äì Professional Scholarship
The Karnataka State Wakf Foundation for Women Development, Bangalore invites applications in the prescribed formats from Muslim Girls students studying in Professional Courses ‚Äì B. E. / M. Tech.
For details visit Website:
www.kswwf.com

,
Govt. of Karnataka awards Defence Scholarships to children of defence personnel.

For details visit Govt. of Karnataka, Dept. of Sainik Welfare & Resettlement Website: www.karnatakasainikwelfare.com

. The Govt. of Karnataka has introduced Arivu (Education loan) to help the minority students with financial assistancetill the completion of the course, for the professional courses like Engineering. Foundation for Academic Excellence and Access (FAEA)

Indian Oil Scholarship Schemes.
600 scholarships are awarded on merit-cum-means basis to support talent among the deserving students belonging to families with less than Rs. 1 lakh gross annual income, who are pursuing professional courses like engineering, and MBA. For details visit the Indian Oil Company Website:

Department of Physical Education & Sports
Vision
To serve the student community for better health and active life style¬† through participation in physical activities and sports.
Mission
To train competent players with specific training.
To inculcate sportsmanship spirit & team work culture.
To ensure women empowerment through sports & physical activities.
About
VDIT
is keen in providing sufficient time and facilities for sports and gymnasium. A physical Director takes care of physical fitness and sporting needs of student. A well- equipped gym is available. VDIT Has facilities for indoor games like table tennis, carom, chess, etc. and for outdoor games such as volleyball, foot ball, Hand ball as well as Kho-Kho, Basketball, Cricket, Athletics and Net Ball etc.

Transportation
Transportation Facilities
Safety of the students is a major concern.
Hence, the transport facility provided by our institution is fully equipped with comfortable seating layout in each of our bus. The college provides excellent transportation facilities with a fleet of 12 buses for students and staff from Hubballi, Dharwad, Dandeli, Belagavi, Alnavar, Khanapur and Beedi. We cover the entire areas of Hubballili and Dharwad in our transportation facility.
The Transportation facility is also provided to the students when students attend pool campus placements, technical workshops, cultural events, competitions etc at other colleges. All the buses are equipped with GPS equipment to track the vehicles and camera in order to ensure safety of the students.
Bus Timings
Belgaum:¬† ¬†7:00 at 3rd Gate
Dharwad:¬† ¬†7: 45 at Srinagar
Hubli:¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬†7:00
Dandeli:¬† ¬† ¬†8:00

Mess/Fast Food
Boys Mess
Girls Mess
College Canteen
Inside the campus of our VDRIT College there are Mess & Two Canteen that function well to serve the students and staff members.
The administration of these Canteen & Mess is given to experienced, proficient and committed contractors.
All these Mess & Canteen is open on all working days. Besides, they provide food at a very nominal price.
Purified water from Reverse Osmosis plant is utilized for cooking and drinking. Hot water is also provided for cooking and drinking purposes.
Timings:
Breakfast ‚Äî>7.00 am to 9.00 am
Lunch ‚Äî>12.45 pm to 1.45 pm
Snacks ‚Äî>4.45 pm to 5.45 pm
Dinner ‚Äî>7.00 pm to 9.00 pm

Umang-2025
Roof Top Rain Water Harvesting
The Rooftop Rain Water Harvesting is¬†the technique through which rain water is captured from the roof catchments and stored in reservoirs. Harvested rain water can be stored in sub-surface ground water reservoir by adopting artificial recharge techniques to meet the household needs through storage in tanks.
1. Need for Rooftop Rain Water Harvesting
1. To meet the ever increasing demand for water
2. To reduce the runoff which chokes the storm drains.
3. To avoid flooding of roads
4. To augment the ground water storage and control decline of water levels
5. To reduce ground water pollution
6. To improve the quality of ground water
7. To reduce the soil erosion
8. To supplement domestic water requirement during summer, drought etc.
Roof top sheets installed in the guest house
Rain water harvesting pond constructed near guest house
Rain water from roof top sheet collected in the chamber
Rain water harvesting pond constructed near guest house
Lake1 with 100MLD¬† near Shiva temple in the KLS VDIT¬†Campus
Lake1 with 100MLD¬† near Shiva temple in the KLS VDIT¬†campus
Rain water from roof top sheet collected in the chamber¬†¬† ¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†Rain water harvesting pond constructed near guest house Lake1 with 100MLD¬† near Shiva temple in the KLS VDIT¬†¬†¬†¬†¬† Lake 2 with 100MLD¬† near boy‚Äôs hostel in the KLS VDIT camp
Conclusion
Because the rain water harvesting as well as the as the 2 lakes present in the VDIT CAMPUS the 7 bore wells are recharged periodically. Hence there is no water scarcity in the campus even during the summer.

Umang-2025
Civil Engineering
Department Virtual Tour
Civil Engineering is one of the oldest disciplines of engineering fields. Civil Engineering is all about infrastructural development and design techniques. The root of civilization is based on civil engineering. If there is no growth in the infrastructure of a country, one cannot think of growth in any sector. One of the greatest engineering legends from India, Sir. M. Vishweshwaryya who has been honored with the knighthood by the queen of England is basically a civil engineer.
Civil Engineers build the world‚Äôs infrastructure. In doing so they quietly shape the History of Nations around the world. To train the students with such qualities, the evergreen Civil engineering department was started for the academic year 2010-2011 with the intake of 60 in KLS‚Äôs VDIT Haliyal.
Department is well equipped with modern instruments to carry out the laboratory experiments.
The department has a library with a good number of books to help the students to upgrade their knowledge in various areas of Civil Engineering.
The department has a student‚Äôs association, ‚ÄúACES‚Äù which conduct Technical Talk, site visit Quiz, Building Model making to encourage the students and to showcase their talents.
Department is headed by Dr. Ashik Bellary along with other eight well-qualified teaching faculty.
Civil Engineering
About the Department

)

Our Vision
‚ÄúTo excel in imparting civil engineering knowledge of global standards in meeting societal and environmental challenges with professional ethics.‚Äù
Our Mission
M1.
To develop
entrepreneurial
and skill and team work among students.
M2.
To inculcate basics of civil engineering knowledge to meet the professional challenges through
research and innovation
in
collaboration with industries.
M3.
To cultivate qualities of professional ethics and commitment towards welfare of the
society
and
environment.
Programme Educational Outcomes
PEO1:
To design and utilize new materials, processes, and projects through research and development for the welfare of society
PEO2:
To communicate feasible technical solutions for civil engineering problems faced by public through presentations and demonstrations.
PEO3:
To enhance the personal knowledge, leadership quality and entrepreneurial skill to succeed in civil engineering profession.
Program Specific Outcomes
PSO1:
Graduates will be able to plan, analyse and design in order to execute and maintain civil engineering structures using alternative materials and innovative construction practices for sustainable infrastructural development of the nation.
PSO2:
Graduates will be able to pursue career opportunities for personal and professional growth by demonstrating leadership skill, professional integrity and solve issues related to civil engineering and allied fields.
Programme Outcomes
Engineering knowledge
: Apply the knowledge of mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals, and an engineering specialization to the solution of complex engineering problems.
Problem analysis
: Identity, formulate, review research literature, and analyze complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using the first principles of mathematics, natural sciences, and engineering sciences.
Design/development of solutions
: Design solutions for complex engineering problems and design system components or processes that meet the specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health and safety and cultural, societal, and environmental considerations.
Conduct investigations of complex problems
: Use research-based knowledge and research methods including design of experiments, analysis, interpretation of data, and synthesis of the information to provide valid conclusions.
Modern tool usage
: Create, select, and apply appropriate techniques, resources, and modern engineering and IT tools including prediction and modeling to complex engineering achieves with an understanding of the limitations.
The engineer and society
: Apply to reason informed by the contextual knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to the professional engineering practice.
Environment and sustainability
: Understand the impact of professional engineering solutions in societal and environmental contexts and demonstrate the knowledge of and need for sustainable development.
Ethics
: Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of the engineering practice.
Individual and team work
: Function effectively as an individual and as a member or leader in diverse teams and in multidisciplinary settings.
Communication
: Communicate effectively on complex engineering activities with the engineering community and with society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations and give and receive clear instructions.
Project management and finance
: Demonstrate knowledge and understanding of the engineering and management principles and apply these to one‚Äôs own work, as a member and leader in a team, to manage projects and in multidisciplinary environments.
Life-long learning
: Recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.

Computer Science and Engineering [AI & ML]
Virtutal Tour
The Department of computer science Engineering AI & ML  was established in the year 2022. The Department is committed to continuously improving the quality of education by enhancing the knowledge of Students & Staff. With the increasing demand for computer science & Technology in the development of software industries, the department has met the requirements with the latest computing machines and software.

Umang-2025
Electronics and Communication Engineering
Department Virtual Tour
The Electronics & Communication Engineering Department was started in the year 2004 and now conducts one undergraduate program (BE) with an intake of 120, one postgraduate program (M.Tech.) in Industrial Electronics with an intake of 18. ECE department is also a VTU recognised research centre where in several candidates are presently involved in active research. A total of 19 experienced faculty members support core specializations like Communication systems, VLSI Design and Embedded Systems, and Signal Processing.
UG & PG students are encouraged to take up interdisciplinary project works in various domains and students are placed in reputed companies namely [Infosys, Wipro, Sankalp semiconductors, Cadence etc].
The department has MOU with various leading industries viz [BSNL, KPTCL, WCT, DASSAULT SYSTEMES etc]
Academics at UG and PG level is sustained with a staff to student ratio as per the NBA guidelines. The curriculum includes mini & major projects to develop the students‚Äô independent analytical abilities.
To support research across the specializations, ECE department is equipped with several hardware and software tools.
Apart from academic research in the core areas, ECE dept. has also established advanced robotics lab in association with IIT Bombay under e-Yantra program. This initiative has facilitated several students to take up their mini/major projects and internship in the field of robotics.
The department also conducts various technical & non-technical events through the ECO platform, which is one of the best platform for students to explore their talents.

Umang-2025
Electrical and Electronics Engineering
Department Virtual Tour
The Department of Electrical & Electronics Engineering was established in the year 2004 with an intake of 60. The department conducts four years Bachelor of Engineering in Electrical & Electronics Engineering degree course affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belagavi. The department has well-qualified staff with expertise in Power Systems, Electronics and Computer Applications, assisted by skilled supporting staff. The department has present state of art laboratories to meet the requirements of University curriculum. The course content includes the basics of Electrical Engineering and a comprehensive treatment on Electrical Machines, Electrical Networks, Power Generation, Transmission and Distribution, Electrical Power Systems, Computer Application to Power System. The course also gives a considerable coverage to Analog & Digital Electronics, Power Electronics and Computer System and applications. The Department library has large volume of technical books, competitive exam books, project reports, Magazines to cater the need of the students. Electrical Staff and Student Association (ELECTRA)-a departmental association provides a platform for students to exhibit their talents in various extracurricular activities. The Department has Institution of Engineers (India) Student Chapter which conducts various technical activities like Expert Talks, Technical Visits, Workshops and Conferences etc. The students graduated from the department gets ample opportunities for securing good placements in Electrical Industries and Electronics and Computer fields.

Mechanical Engineering

Mechanical Engineering
Mechanical Engineering
Department Virtual Tour
Mechanical Engineering Department
started with the B.E. Programme in the year 2004. It is affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University (VTU), Belagavi, Karnataka. Since its inception, the department has been actively involved in imparting quality education to the students.
The Department has highly qualified, committed and motivated faculty. It has well equipped spacious Laboratories and other Infrastructural facilities to cater the needs of budding Mechanical Engineering students.
The departmental library has a sound collection of books including reference books & text books. The post graduate programme was started in the year 2013 in Thermal Engineering with 18 students intake. The department is recognized as a Research Centre of VTU.
Over the decade, the department has established state-of-the art laboratories in various subjects which are utilized both by undergraduate and post-graduate students for conducting experiments.
The department has MOUs with various sectors of industry ranging from automotive to manufacturing domains.
Mechanical Engineering
About the Department
Our Faculty
Student‚Äôs Association
Research
Awards Appreciations
Professional Body Membership
Gallery
Our Vision
To provide value based education in the field of mechanical engineering for the society where the best of teaching, learning, research and consultancy synergize to face the global market.
Our Mission
To impart innovative knowledge and skills that enhances quality education.
To strengthen collaboration with industry, government and R&D institutes.
To develop abilities to cater the society needs through sustainable scientific approach.
Programme Educational Outcomes
PEO 1: Graduate will update themselves through lifelong learning such as higher studies, skill enhancement and other professional activities.
PEO 2: Establish a successful career in mechanical engineering and related fields in industry and other organization where an engineering approach to problem solving is highly valued.
PEO 3: Graduates will contribute to society through their devotion in science and technology leading to uplift their standard of living.
PEO 4: Contribute significantly in a multidisciplinary work environment with ethical standards by understanding the role of mechanical engineering.
Program Specific Outcomes
PSO1 : Analyze, design and develop machining systems to solve the engineering problems by integrating thermal, design and manufacturing domains of mechanical engineering.
PSO2 : Adopt a multidisciplinary approach to solve real-time industrial problems.
Programme Outcomes
Engineering knowledge
: Apply the knowledge of mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals, and an engineering specialization to the solution of complex engineering problems.
Problem analysis
: Identity, formulate, review research literature, and analyze complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using the first principles of mathematics, natural sciences, and engineering sciences.
Design/development of solutions
: Design solutions for complex engineering problems and design system components or processes that meet the specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health and safety and cultural, societal, and environmental considerations.
Conduct investigations of complex problems
: Use research-based knowledge and research methods including design of experiments, analysis, interpretation of data, and synthesis of the information to provide valid conclusions.
Modern tool usage
: Create, select, and apply appropriate techniques, resources, and modern engineering and IT tools including prediction and modeling to complex engineering achieves with an understanding of the limitations.
The engineer and society
: Apply to reason informed by the contextual knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to the professional engineering practice.
Environment and sustainability
: Understand the impact of professional engineering solutions in societal and environmental contexts and demonstrate the knowledge of and need for sustainable development.
Ethics
: Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of the engineering practice.
Individual and team work
: Function effectively as an individual and as a member or leader in diverse teams and in multidisciplinary settings.
Communication
: Communicate effectively on complex engineering activities with the engineering community and with society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations and give and receive clear instructions.
Project management and finance
: Demonstrate knowledge and understanding of the engineering and management principles and apply these to one‚Äôs own work, as a member and leader in a team, to manage projects and in multidisciplinary environments.
Life-long learning
: Recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.

Department of Mathematics
Department of Mathematics was established in the year 2004 and has experienced, dedicated and skilled faculties who are specialized in diverse areas of mathematics such as algebra, calculus, analysis and many more mathematical concepts. The department has 4 faculties having more than 10 years of experience. Department consists of one Associate Professor and 3 Assistant Professors. Faculties attend various conferences, seminars, workshops regularly to enrich their knowledge, which benefit students in greater aspects.
Faculties are involved in regular counselling of the students and guide students in boosting their mathematical skills. Through Aptitude and Quizzes the Department is boosting the students mathematical skills.
Department of Mathematics offers Ph.D. program affiliated under Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belagavi. Research Scholars are pursuing Ph.D. on various Mathematical domains under the VTU Research Supervisors. We have more than 26 research publications in the UGC recognized Journals. We also conduct the presentation on the research topics by the research scholars to encourage them to have continuity in the research aspects.

Department of Chemistry
Department of Chemistry is established in the year 2004 to offer basic principles of chemistry with a focus on applied aspects to undergraduate engineering students.¬† The department has always accomplished the best results at University examinations. ¬†The strength of the department is sincere and dedicated team of highly qualified and experienced faculty with affection for teaching and research.
The department aims at instilling a sense of keen observation and analysis in the minds of students, instigate the analytical skills in students and help the students excel in academic standards.¬† The department also aspires to develop a full-fledged Research and Development Center in Chemistry, cultivating an inclination in students / staff to take up research, which will be of help to the industries and society at large.
The department is recognized as ‚ÄúResearch Center‚Äù in the year 2010 and offers Ph.D./M.Sc.(Engg.) program by research, which is affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belagavi.

Industrial Electronics
Outline
AICTE
has granted permission to start M.Tech course in¬†Industrial Electronics¬†under the department of Electronics and Communication Department from the academic year 2011 ‚Äì 12 with an intake of 18 students. The course is affiliated to VTU, Belgaum. Students having Bachelor‚Äôs Degree in ECE,EEE,TCE and IEE can take this course.
M.Tech. Industrial Electronics is¬† a¬† postgraduate Electronics Engineering course. Industrial Electronic Engineering unites the characteristics of two basic areas of knowledge, namely Automation and Industrial Electronics. It is a growing discipline that is increasingly becoming more competitive in the market. It is¬† essentially Electronics Engineering with specialization in control and automation. This course gives importance to industrial applications of electronics and motivates students to explore new horizons. The course mainly deals with areas like Power Electronics, Industrial Electronics, Control Systems, Communication Systems and Industrial Automation. It also includes a detailed study of Microprocessors and microcontrollers with their applications.
How is M.Tech. Industrial Electronics Course Beneficial?
The course gives a deeper and complete scientific information in the Industrial Electronics area, but¬†also it is strongly linked to industrial sectors, given the vast experience of the teaching staff R&D¬†projects with companies, with its corresponding impact on the master classes.
There is ample scope for starting small scale industries as well.

Umang-2025
Thermal Engineering
Outline
This programme aims at necessary analytical and technical competence in various aspects of Thermal Power Engineering. Thermal Power plants have an increasingly dominant role to play in the vital power generation sector.
AICTE has granted permission to start M.Tech course in Thermal Power Engineering under the department of Mechanical Engineering from the academic year 2013 ‚Äì 14 with an intake of 18 students. The course is affiliated to VTU, Belgaum. Students having Bachelor‚Äôs Degree in Mechanical Engineering / Industrial Production Engineering / Manufacturing Engineering or equivalent degree; AMIE in appropriate branch can join this P G Program.
The stream of specialization of Thermal Engineering offers courses related to theory and applications of thermal engineering. The Thermal Engineering course lays emphasis on real- time applications of fluid flow, Heat Transfer in thermal energy systems, refrigeration and Air Conditioning Systems, I. C Engines and non- conventional energy resources. The core courses are designed to provide the students the required base for undertaking specialized electives and the project in the fields of heat transfer, Fluid Dynamics, Thermal Design and development of various components. The lab activities are designed in consultation with industries and research activities.
Facilities
Research Lab is well equipped with modern innovative equipment like:
The Thermal Imager (FLUKE TI- 400) measures the temperature from 20
o
C to 1200
o
C by identifying the long wave radiation.
The ELGI (E07En)‚ÄùScrew Air Compressor‚Äù provides compressed air system to the laboratory to carry out the projects.
The regulator DC power supply servers the purpose of supplying uniform heat flux to test surface.
Variable compression ratio petrol engine test rig with swinging field DC generator
Wind Tunnels

Electronics and Communication Engineering
Objectives
Research Activities including Basic, Strategic, and Applied Research is undertaken for solving real-life problems.
Research Projects of Students at Undergraduate, Postgraduate, and Ph.D. Scholars have undertaken it as part of the curriculum or for additional enrichment.
Organizing and Conducting Motivational Talks, Seminars by Eminent Personalities for the students and faculty fraternity.
Preparation, Compilation, and Submission of Students and Faculty Research Project Proposals to a variety of Funding Agencies and to execute them well within deadlines.
Publications, Presentations, and Communication of the Research Outcomes to the external World.
Scholarly activities intended to expand knowledge boundaries by analysis, synthesis, and interpretation of ideas and information by making use of rigorous methodologies.
Preparation of¬† Theoretical on-paper designs, software simulations, prototype developments, experimentations, analyses, and documentation in the form of technical reports.

Research Centre in Mechanical Engineering
The department is recognized as ‚ÄúResearch Center‚Äù in the year 2014-15 and offers Ph.D./ M.Sc.(Engg.) program by research, which is affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belgaum. The faculty members are actively involved in research activities. Major areas of research are thermal and fluids engineering, lean manufacturing, and Jet impingement.
Faculty members have published many research papers in their respective fields in international journals of high impact factors and have presented a good number of papers in national / international conferences and seminars.

Department of Physics
Research, Development and Innovation
Department of Physics
The department is recognized as ‚ÄúResearch Center‚Äù in the year 2015 and offers Ph.D./ M.Sc.(Engg.) program by research, which is affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belagavi, vide VTU letter no. VTU/Aca-Res-Cen./2015-16/6502(f) dated 21-10-2015.
The faculty members are actively involved in research activities. Major areas of research are vibrational spectroscopy, DFT calculations, Semiconductors, Nano-materials, Condensed matter physics, Laser spectroscopy and Transport properties of Dilute magnetic semiconductors and thin films.
Faculty members have published 15 research papers in their respective fields in international journals and have presented a good number of papers in national / international conferences and seminars.
Applications are invited for registration to Full time / Part time Ph.D. Programs in Physics as per prevailing regulations of Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belgaum. Eligibility Criteria for enrolment to Ph.D. is as per VTU rules available on the link:
http://research.vtu.ac.in/Research/index.html

Mathematics Research Center
Department of Mathematics was established in the year 2004. At present there are totally 4 experienced faculties in the department out of which two faculty members are VTU recognized Research Supervisors. Department of Mathematics is being recognized as Research Center by VTU, Belagavi in the year 2011 and permission has been granted to guide the research scholars. Department is well equipped with infrastructure facilities like computers, Internet facility, printers, reference books etc.

Training and Placement Cell
The Training & Placement cell is here to help you understand your strengths, weakness, and interests, and guide you through the process of exploring various career options. It is important that you start planning for your career early. We offer a variety of student-centric services that complement classroom learning to prepare students for careers in industry, entrepreneurship, research or further study. The Training & Placement cell functions across all academic departments and offers placement assistance.
Contact Us
Prof. Rajat Acharya
Director ‚Äì Training & Placement
E-mail: placement@klsvdit.edu.in
Phone: +91-9482294805
Our Vision
To be the preferred choice of top corporate in India for Campus recruitment by consistently updating and upgrading the competencies of students, matching the needs of the corporate sector thereby creating value for all the stakeholders.
Our Mission
To empower students to meet Industry and Societal Challenges.
To help the undergraduate and postgraduate students through counseling, instructions, and training for the development of desired skills essential for suitable job profile/higher education/self-employment.
Invite the Corporate Industries/Research or Academic Institutes/Commercial Organizations/ Public Sector Undertakings for campus placement.
Provide opportunities to all the students, to interact with corporate executives, and to prepare them on industry required skills from time to time.

Vibration & Thermography Monitoring
Vision
The Vision of Vibration and Thermography Consultancy at
KLS, Vishwanathrao Deshpande Institute of Technology, Haliyal
with
Diagnostic Engineers, Bangalore
is to make students Industry Ready, corporate training for Industries / Faculties and Consultancy for Industries in the area of Vibration and Thermography. The consultancy will be Mentored / Guided under the leadership of
Mr. Madhusudan N, Vibration Analyst, CAT‚ÄìII, ISO Certified, Diagnostic Engineers, Bangalore
.¬† ¬†He has got rich experience in the area of Condition Monitoring for more than 21 years covering various sectors like
Power sector, Steel Sector, Petroleum Oil / Refineries & Automotive Sector
. The KLS VDIT will be the
first college to start Proficiency Center
with Industry Connect in North Karnataka & North Kannada.
Why Vibration Monitoring and Thermography ?
Vibration monitoring is process of noticing a change in displacement/velocity/acceleration in rotating machine. Using FFT analyzer, the signals are collected in three different directions i.e. horizontal, vertical & axial directions. The centrifugal forces are increased at faulty location thus seen increase in amplitude at certain frequency. The overview of vibration monitoring is shown in figure 1,
Thermography is an excellent condition monitoring tool to assist in reduction of maintenance costs of the system. This technique allows for the monitoring of temperatures and thermal patterns while the equipment is online and running under full load. Most mechanical equipment has allowable operating temperature limits that can be used as guidelines. Infrared Thermal Imaging can be used on a wide variety of equipment including pumps, motors, bearings, pulleys, fans, drives, conveyors etc. Infrared Thermal Imaging enhances a company‚Äôs ability to predict equipment failure and plan corrective action before a costly shutdown or equipment damage.

Why Our Services?
Because we have mentor of 21 years of experience in,
Vibration Data collection, Data interpretation, diagnosis and trending of rotating machines.
Hands on experience on usage of vibration data collectors for Vibration Monitoring of mechanical equipments.
Rotating machines on-site balancing.
Trouble shooting of rotating machines(misalignment,looseness,bent shaft etc)
Natural frequency measurements of turbine blades.
Sound spectrum analysis.
Thermal Analysis.
Responsibilities Performed Till Date
Schedule based Vibration Monitoring of Rotating equipment‚Äôs (Annual maintenance contract) for¬†¬†¬† auto, oil refineries paper mills, pharmacy and process industries.
Vibration analysis and on-site balancing of turbine-gearbox-generator assembly at power plants.
Handled several TG sets starting from 2 MW to 150 MW sets.
Vibration studies and on-site balancing of paint shop blowers, fans, stand-alone generator assembly, motor assembly, Horizontal machining centre, vertical machining centre.
Hands on experience in Analysis like Equipment‚Äôs Unbalance, Misalignment, Mechanical Looseness, Bearing failures, Blade pass-Vane pass, Gears & Belt related problems.
Bump tests performed on rotating machinery components like couplings, turbine blades, pulleys etc to know the resonance band/critical speeds.
Major Assignments Handled Till Date
Vibration studies and diagnosis of 2X25 MW gas turbine power plant at BAFA, Bahrain.
Vibration measurements and on-site balancing of high speed spindles which runs at 30000 rpm.
Blade natural frequency tests for 150, 230 MW turbines at National Thermal Power Corporation India.
Shaft failure analysis and investigation for HCL technologies.
Handled several vibration studies and on-site balancing assignments for Toyodenki power systems (In Collaboration with Toyodenki Japan) high capacity generators starting from 8 to 35 MW sets.
On-site balancing of 54 ton generator rotor-motor assembly at Central Power Research Institute, Bangalore, India.
Vibration measurements and trouble shooting of 30 MW Gas Turbine Gearbox-compressor train, Doha offshore at one of the leading Petroleum refinery in Qatar.
Vibration studies and analysis of 2 X 2.5 MW Hydro machines for Boving Fouress at Srilanka &Vibration studies and on-site balancing of 60 MW Hydro generator at Sabarigiri power station, India (First of its kind high capacity hydro station in India).
Rotor dynamic support for handling vibration problems in a 35 MW TG set at one of the sugar mills (Software used: XL Rotor).
Failure investigation and reporting of a Demag compressor blades at Tata Steels, Jemshedpur, India
Vibration studies and on-site balancing of motor-generator-flywheel assembly. Weight of the flywheel was 16 tons and runs at 1500/1800 rpm. This machine was first of its kind developed in India for short circuit testing and analysis.
Corporate training on vibration basics and condition monitoring at Caledonian College of Engineering, Oman.

Research & IPR
Umang-2025
Internal Quality Assurance Cell
The primary aim of IQAC is to develop a system for conscious, consistent and catalytic action to improve the academic and administrative performance of the institution. It also promotes the measures for institutional functioning towards quality enhancement through internalization of quality culture and institutionalization of best practices.
Objectives:
The Primary aim of the IQAC is to develop a system for conscious, consistent and catalytic action to improve the academic and administrative performance of the College.
The IQAC will provide greater clarity and focus in institutional functioning towards quality enhancement and facilitate internalization of the quality culture.
The IQAC will contribute towards enhancement and integration among the activities of the College and institutionalize many good practices.
IQAC evolve mechanisms and procedures for:
Ensuring timely, efficient and progressive performance of academic, administrative and financial tasks
The relevance and quality of academic and research programmes
Equitable access to and affordability of academic¬† programmes for various sections of society
Optimization and integration of modern methods of teaching and learning
The credibility of evaluation procedures
Ensuring the adequacy, maintenance and functioning of the support structure and services
Research sharing and networking with other institutions in India and abroad
Functions of the IQAC:
Development and application of quality benchmarks/parameters for various academic and administrative activities of the institution
Facilitating the creation of a learner-centric environment conducive to quality education and faculty maturation to adopt the required knowledge and technology for participatory teaching and learning process
Arrangement for feedback response from students, parents and other stakeholders on quality-related institutional processes
Organization of inter and intra institutional workshops, seminars on quality related themes and promotion of quality circles
Acting as a nodal agency of the Institution for coordinating quality-related activities.
Development of Quality Culture in the institution
Periodical conduct of Academic and Administrative Audit and its follow-up.
As per the guidelines of AICTE, Internal Quality Assurance Cell (IQAC), formed in our institution which comprise of one management member, one industrialist, three to eight teaching staff, one administrative staff, and two students. The structure of IQAC at KLS, VDIT, Haliyal is as follows:
