Research & IPR
Umang-2025
Research & IPR
Vision
To advance human knowledge and contribute to the betterment of society through cutting-edge research and innovation.Ôªø
Mission
1. Foster a culture of curiosity and intellectual exploration, encouraging interdisciplinary collaboration to drive breakthrough discoveries.
2.Cultivate a team of dedicated professionals who demonstrate unwavering commitment to ethical research practices and promote entrepreneurial thinking.
3.Forge robust partnerships with industry leaders and seek global collaborations to drive innovation and technological advancement.
4.Promote a sense of social responsibility among researchers and instill a commitment to address pressing societal challenges.
5.Focus on comprehensive, sustainable development by conducting research that aligns with the principles of economic, environmental, and social responsibility.
Objectives
Interdisciplinary Collaboration
: Foster interdisciplinary research teams to tackle complex problems and promote knowledge exchange across various fields.
Ethical Research Practices:
Ensure that all research and development activities adhere to the highest ethical standards, including responsible data usage, informed consent, and transparency.
Entrepreneurial Thinking:
Encourage researchers to explore innovative ideas and potential commercial applications of their work, fostering an entrepreneurial mindset within the organization.
Industry Partnerships:
Establish strong and mutually beneficial partnerships with industry leaders to leverage resources, share knowledge, and facilitate the translation of research into practical applications.
Global Collaborations:
Actively seek collaborations with international institutions and researchers to gain diverse perspectives, share expertise, and contribute to global research initiatives.
Addressing Societal Challenges:
Prioritize research projects that directly address pressing societal challenges, such as healthcare disparities, environmental sustainability, and technological inequality.
Sustainable Development:
Conduct research that aligns with principles of economic, environmental, and social responsibility, with a focus on sustainable solutions and practices.
Innovation and Technological Advancement:
Strive for breakthrough discoveries and the development of cutting-edge technologies that contribute to the betterment of society.
Continuous Learning and Skill Development:
Invest in the professional development of the research team, providing opportunities for ongoing education and skill enhancement to stay at the forefront of their respective fields.
Community Engagement:
Promote a sense of social responsibility among researchers by engaging with the local community and actively participating in outreach programs that address local needs and concerns.
Publication and Knowledge Sharing:
Encourage researchers to publish their findings in reputable journals and share knowledge through conferences and public engagement to contribute to the advancement of human knowledge.
Measurable Impact:
Establish key performance indicators and metrics to assess the impact of research and development activities on society, the environment, and the economy, ensuring accountability and continuous improvement.
Resource Allocation:
Efficiently allocate resources, including funding and personnel, to support research projects that align with the organization‚Äôs mission and strategic goals.
Inclusivity and Diversity:
Promote a diverse and inclusive research environment to ensure a wide range of perspectives and ideas are considered in the research and development process.
Long-Term Vision:
Develop a long-term strategic roadmap that aligns with the vision and mission, outlining how the organization plans to contribute to the betterment of society through research and innovation over the coming years.

Cultural
Activities
University Level Elocution Competition
VTU had conducted regional level elocution competition on 22/12/2022 on the topic
‚ÄúImpact of NEP on Technical Education‚Äù.
This competition was held in online mode , where college recorded speech of best 3 students from our college and uploaded it to the mentioned google drive. Hence in this regional level competition Miss.Sanjana Shivpurmath of 3rd semester E&C department stood 1st place and received a certificate and collection of books.
Miss.Sanjana shivpurmath of 3rd semester E&C department has won 1st place in speech competition conducted by VTU on 22nd December 2022.
ABVP Cultural Fest-Mysore
ABVP had organized two days State level cultural fest at Karnataka state open university, Mysore on 13
th
and 14
th
May 2022.The students of VDIT participated.
Our students won 2
nd
prize in State level Classical group dance competition.
AAVISHKAAR 2K22
:
A one day techno cultural event and a flagship event of VDIT was conducted on 11
th
June 2022, where in more than 5 neighbouring Engineering colleges with more than 400 students have actively participated in various technical events and also in cultural events. Nearly 35-40 participants participated in¬† singing , dance and group dance events.

About Library
Vision
To provide a student friendly learning environment that facilitates dissemination of knowledge using modern tools.
Mission
To provide comprehensive resources and services to support research, teaching and learning needs of the user community.
To augment and maintain collections in the support of the academic pursuits of the college.
‚ÄúEducation is not the amount of information that is put into your brain and runs not there, undigested, all your life. We must have life-building, man-making, character-building, assimilating fine ideas and making them your life and character, you have more education than any man who has got by heart a whole library‚Äù.
‚Ä¶‚Ä¶.. Swami Vivekananda
As Swami Vivekananda said the Library is temple of knowledge it is store house of information, where the user can get desired information. VDIT Library & Information Center is located in spacious building with area of 655sqm.
The Library follows an open access system. Books are classified and cataloged according to the Dewey Decimal Classification and are arranged accordingly.
Features:
Ultra- modern Library provides the best of facilities for all- round development of students.
A marvelous collection of over 46490 volumes that include 6493 titles and more than 8000 reference books.
Subscribing to 52 National journals and International   Journals subscribed through VTU Consortium.
Availability of Spacious reading rooms.
Member of DELNET ,VTU consortium and NDLI.
An investment of 1.12Cr subscription to books and journals.
Lending Library Scheme which facilitates every student with 5 books per semester.
Language Lab for learning  fluent English .
Resources Arrangement: All resources are classified and arranged as per the Dewey Decimal Classification Scheme.

Digital Library
E-Resources :
Click Here
VDIT Institute and Library & Information Center is established in 2004. A library is a temple of knowledge, which blesses its users with the required information and helps them enrich their knowledge. VDIT Library has its own mission to fulfil all sorts of information needs of the students, faculty, and staff of VDIT.
Now VDIT Library has a separate building on campus and is named ‚ÄúJNAN SUDHA‚Äù. The new library building ‚ÄúJNAN SUDHA‚Äù is inaugurated by SHRI. S.GOPALKRISHNAN (Kris) Executive Co-Chairman, Infosys Technologies Ltd., Bengaluru, and Digital Library are inaugurated by SHRI. U. RAMADAS KAMAT Associate Vice President, Infosys Technologies Ltd. Bengaluru, on 02nd June 2012. Area of the Library is 655sqm. The Library Jnan Sudha has subscribed E- Resources through VTU Consortium .
Digital Library/Language Lab
Jnan Sudha has separate Browsing Center for Digital Library; it has 30 high end multimedia systems with high speed internet connectivity. Users can browse the Digital Library, e-Resources and can view multimedia resources. Jnan Sudha is also a member of DELNET and NDLI . Even users can take benefit of Language Lab, they can learn English, German, French and Japanese. The Library is available for reading from 8.00AM. to 8.00PM.

Transportation ‚Äì KLS, VISHWANATHRAO DESHPANDE INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, HALIYAL
Transportation ‚Äì KLS, VISHWANATHRAO DESHPANDE INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, HALIYAL
KLS, VISHWANATHRAO DESHPANDE INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, HALIYAL
Knowledge is Power
Transportation Facilities
Bus Timings
Transportation Facilities
Safety of the students is a major concern.
Hence, the transport facility provided by our institution is fully equipped with comfortable seating layout in each of our bus. The college provides excellent transportation facilities with a fleet of 12 buses for students and staff from Hubballi, Dharwad, Dandeli, Belagavi, Alnavar, Khanapur and Beedi. We cover the entire areas of Hubballili and Dharwad in our transportation facility.
The Transportation facility is also provided to the students when students attend pool campus placements, technical workshops, cultural events, competitions etc at other colleges. All the buses are equipped with GPS equipment to track the vehicles and camera in order to ensure safety of the students.

Umang-2025
ACES
In order to enhance technical skills of the students of Civil Engineering Department, a Technical Association is formed in the Academic year 2011-12 with the name ‚ÄòACES‚Äô-Association of Civil Engineering Students, with a punch line ‚Äú Where Imagination & Reality are Bridged Together‚Äù.
Logo Description
The background of this logo describes major responsibilities being a Civil Engineer. Our Logo illustrates our Foundation and Focus.
A Surveyor in the background is planning for a building before construction, which indicates proper vision and mission for any progress of work.
Prosperous Nation comes up with Intelligent minds, Good infrastructure, Good network of roads and by constructing bridges to overcome obstacles. Our Association ‚ÄòACES‚Äô Trains the students through various events, seminars, study tour etc‚Ä¶ and make them fit To achieve the above dreams for the welfare of the society.
The Green Leaves at the forefront of the logo is a fitting symbol of Eco friendly growth.
Objectives
It aims to improve the student standard with Practical knowledge.
The Association caters the needs of students & provides a forum for developing new technology.
It aims to nurture well disciplined socially committed and technically competent Engineers with innovative thinking.
It proposes to organize various seminars, Lecture, Industrial Visit etc.
‚ÄúSound Body Sound Mind‚Äù Association aims to conduct various sports activity in order to show their talents and make them fit.

‚ÄúPRACTICAL ASPECTS IN CIVIL ENGINEERING‚Äù
An Alumni interaction and site visit was organised in association with Indian Geotechnical Society (IGS) and Institutions Innovation Counsil (IIC) by the Department of Civil Engineering on 07¬†th¬†Feb, 2024 from 11:00am to 1:00pm. The resource person for this event was our proud alumni Er. Sandeep Mirashi, Managing Director, Shravya Constructions, Haliyal (201 1-2015) batch student.
BIS-INDUSTRY VISIT TO ‚ÄúCONECC INDUSTRY PVT LTD, DHARWAD.‚Äù
An industry visit to Conecc Industries Pvt Ltd. Dharwad was organised in association with
Bureau of Indian Standards (BIS) Hubballi
by the Department of Civil Engineering on
28
th
June, 2024 from 10:00am to 12:00pm
.
Shri. Amit Metri, Manager,
Conecc Industries Pvt Ltd. Dharwad
,
interacted with all the ¬†¬†¬†6th semester students of Civil Engineering. During the interaction session, he explained the process of manufacturing the light weight block at his plant. The plant mainly consists of two silos where, the different raw materials are mixed and collected in the container. The container along with mixture is cooled and transported to cutting unit where the sample is cut into four different sizes. At the end, blocks are cured by steam curing method in a closed container for 8hrs. Immediately after curing the light weight blocks are transported to construction sites for various construction purposes.
Even the industry visit helped the students to know the importance of IS standards. Students were briefed about ethical principal and its importance while manufacturing the blocks to maintain the quality.
An educational site visit to Alnavar Railway Station (LWR)
An educational site visit to Alnavar Railway Station (LWR) Alnavar Taluk, Dharwad district was organized by the Department of Civil Engineering for 6
th
semester students on 3
rd
June 2024. The visit was organized successfully with the prior permission of Station Superintendent, Alnavar Railway Station (LWR), under the guidance of our beloved Principal Dr. V. A. Kulkarni and by the initiative and persistent efforts of Head of Department Dr. Ashik Bellary.
The 6
th
semester 30 students, along with Prof. Harsha A. Jadhav and ¬†Prof. Harshvardhan V. S visited Alnavar Railway Station (LWR). During the visit students got knowledge about permanent ways, components of permanent way, Fittings and fastenings, switching point and cross-checking of track levels. Prof. Harsha Jadhav briefed about technical components of railway tracks, different gauges and maintenance of tracks. Mr.Gopalji, Station Master and his team explained about the features of Alnavar railway station, which consist of two railway track and also Alnavar railway station is a junction. The team explained about railway track maintenance with straight edge and level tubes. Prof. Harshvardhan V.S briefed about steel components across the plat form. From this visit, our students got practical exposure of what they learnt in their academics.

C-Force
C ‚Äì force was the name coined for the association of the Computer Science Department‚Äôs people. C- Force was formed on 22/04/2007 to provide a platform for students to express their various curricular & Co-curricular activities. It also encourages the students to participate in state/ National level Technical events. C-force has organized various events.

ECO  Activities
ECO was started on 12th September 2007 with the intention to provide a platform for the students to exhibit their talents. This association was started in order to involve students in various curricular and co-curricular activities and also for the overall growth of the department. Also under this association, various activities will be conducted, by the students in coordination with the staff.
The various activities conducted by ECO are as follows.
Short-Term Training Program(STTP) For Diploma Students From 26.12.2018 to 5.1.2019
Workshop on Arduino and IOT October 2018

Mission of Electra:
To provide a platform to all the talents within, encourage, nurture, and see to that every student of EEE emerges out to confident, inspired, the responsible citizen of India and always prepared to face the challenges, spring up as the win.

The Association activities for the year 2015 ‚Äì 16
Students of 6th semester underwent 7 days and 3 days training in Shantala Transformers, Hubli and Patil Electricals, Hubli respectively.
Alumni meet for all the passed out students was organized on 23rd April, 2016. Alumni members interacted with the students about present industrial scenario.
Students had attended the online Sci Lab Test on 15th April, 2016, conducted by IIT, Bombay in which 5 students successfully cleared the exam.
Volley Ball and Chess competitions were organised in college level during April, 2016.
Cartoon Sketching and Paper Crafting competitions were organised in college level during April, 2016.
Department had organised the Technical Aptitude Test on DC Machines and Transformer & Induction Machines on 17th and 24th March 2016.
Technical events were organised during Tech. Fest ‚ÄúAavishkar-2016‚Äù between 22nd and 24th Feb., 2016. The events were namely; Tribology, Bhaago Dundo Banao and Paper Presentation.
2nd year students registered for online NPTEL Course on Fundamentals of Electrical Material and Devices on 16th Feb., 2016.
Department had organised the online Sci Lab Workshop for pre-final year students on 9th Feb.,2016.
A visit to Hydro Power Plant, Ganesh Gudi was organised for Pre-final year students as a part of Industrial Trip during Jan.,2016.
An Aptitude Test was conducted on 2nd Nov.,2015 for the students of all branches.

Mechanical Mesa
MESA
Mechanical Engineering Students Association has started in the year 2006, with an intension of providing platform for the students to exhibit their co-curricular talent.
With the guidance of staff MESA has conducted various earmark able events. Marathon in 2011 to pay homage to TSUNAMI victims of Japan.
Innovision: In 2012 competition among the students in various categories like Admaking, Photovision, Vision walk, Media mind, Innoshop,  Stunt mania etc.
Technical talks, Cricket tournament, Badminton are the few other events to name.
MESA has become a major student association in the institute to encourage and participate in the cultural, sports and technical events.
MESA has conducted many Technical talks by the subject experts, Industry persons and organized industrial visits for the benefit of students.

Computer Science and Engineering
About Department
Department Virtual Tour
The Department of computer science Engineering was established in the year 2004. The Department is committed to continuously improving the quality of education by enhancing the knowledge of Students & Staff. With the increasing demand for computer science & Technology in the development of software industries, the department has met the requirements with the latest computing machines and software.
The department is well equipped with more than 500 computers with the latest configuration and with all the necessary software.
The department has a student‚Äôs association, ‚ÄúC- Force‚Äù which conducts competitive technical events under the guidance/ vigilance of faculty.
The department has a library with a good number of books and magazines to help the students to upgrade their knowledge in various areas of computer science and Engineering applications.
The department has well qualified & experienced staff members.
Through the interaction with the industry‚Äôs latest developments and trends, the department has created the right ambiance for learning with exposure to live projects & in-plant training.

Our Vision
To achieve excellence in¬†technical education,  research,¬† and innovation¬†in computer science and Engineering by emphasizing on global trending technologies.
Our Mission
To train students with conceptual understanding through¬†innovative pedagogies.
To imbibe professional, research, and¬†entrepreneurial skills¬†with a commitment to the nation‚Äôs development at large.
To¬†strengthen the industry-institute¬†Interaction.
To promote life‚Äìlong learning with a sense of¬†societal & ethical¬†responsibilities.
Programme Educational Outcomes
To develop an ability to identify and analyze the requirements of Computer Science and Engineering in design and provide novel engineering solutions.
To develop abilities to work in a team on multidisciplinary projects with effective communication skills, ethical qualities, and leadership roles.
To develop abilities for a successful Computer Science Engineer and achieve higher career goals.
Program Specific Outcomes
To develop abilities to model real world problems using¬†appropriate algorithms, computational theories and programming languages in the area of Computer Science and Engineering.
To develop an ability to inculcate innovation, entrepreneurial and leadership skills.
Programme Outcomes
Engineering knowledge
: Apply the knowledge of mathematics, science, engineering fundamentals, and an engineering specialization to the solution of complex engineering problems.
Problem analysis
: Identity, formulate, review research literature, and analyze complex engineering problems reaching substantiated conclusions using the first principles of mathematics, natural sciences, and engineering sciences.
Design/development of solutions
: Design solutions for complex engineering problems and design system components or processes that meet the specified needs with appropriate consideration for public health and safety and cultural, societal, and environmental considerations.
Conduct investigations of complex problems
: Use research-based knowledge and research methods including design of experiments, analysis, interpretation of data, and synthesis of the information to provide valid conclusions.
Modern tool usage
: Create, select, and apply appropriate techniques, resources, and modern engineering and IT tools including prediction and modeling to complex engineering achieves with an understanding of the limitations.
The engineer and society
: Apply to reason informed by the contextual knowledge to assess societal, health, safety, legal and cultural issues and the consequent responsibilities relevant to the professional engineering practice.
Environment and sustainability
: Understand the impact of professional engineering solutions in societal and environmental contexts and demonstrate the knowledge of and need for sustainable development.
Ethics
: Apply ethical principles and commit to professional ethics and responsibilities and norms of the engineering practice.
Individual and team work
: Function effectively as an individual and as a member or leader in diverse teams and in multidisciplinary settings.
Communication
: Communicate effectively on complex engineering activities with the engineering community and with society at large, such as being able to comprehend and write effective reports and design documentation, make effective presentations and give and receive clear instructions.
Project management and finance
: Demonstrate knowledge and understanding of the engineering and management principles and apply these to one‚Äôs own work, as a member and leader in a team, to manage projects and in multidisciplinary environments.
Life-long learning
: Recognize the need for, and have the preparation and ability to engage in independent and life-long learning in the broadest context of technological change.

Industrial Electronics ‚Äì KLS, VISHWANATHRAO DESHPANDE INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, HALIYAL
Industrial Electronics ‚Äì KLS, VISHWANATHRAO DESHPANDE INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, HALIYAL
KLS, VISHWANATHRAO DESHPANDE INSTITUTE OF TECHNOLOGY, HALIYAL
Knowledge is Power
Industrial
electronics
Outline
facilities
Outline
Outline
AICTE
has granted permission to start M.Tech course in¬†Industrial Electronics¬†under the department of Electronics and Communication Department from the academic year 2011 ‚Äì 12 with an intake of 18 students. The course is affiliated to VTU, Belgaum. Students having Bachelor‚Äôs Degree in ECE,EEE,TCE and IEE can take this course.
M.Tech. Industrial Electronics is¬† a¬† postgraduate Electronics Engineering course. Industrial Electronic Engineering unites the characteristics of two basic areas of knowledge, namely Automation and Industrial Electronics. It is a growing discipline that is increasingly becoming more competitive in the market. It is¬† essentially Electronics Engineering with specialization in control and automation. This course gives importance to industrial applications of electronics and motivates students to explore new horizons. The course mainly deals with areas like Power Electronics, Industrial Electronics, Control Systems, Communication Systems and Industrial Automation. It also includes a detailed study of Microprocessors and microcontrollers with their applications.
How is M.Tech. Industrial Electronics Course Beneficial?
The course gives a deeper and complete scientific information in the Industrial Electronics area, but¬†also it is strongly linked to industrial sectors, given the vast experience of the teaching staff R&D¬†projects with companies, with its corresponding impact on the master classes.
There is ample scope for starting small scale industries as well.
M.Tech. Industrial Electronics Employment Areas
Academic Institutions
R&D Departments
Manufacturing Industries
Automobile Companies
Aeronautics
Fabrication & Designing Companies

Umang-2025
Best Practices
Title 1: Value Added Service to Society
Objective
To create Awareness about Technology to the rural mass.
To Spread Nationalism, Human values and Life Ethics among Students and General Public.
The Context:
Higher Education Institutions not only contribute in providing technical skilled talent to the country, but also act as catalyst in enhancing life standards and life values among students, parents and public at large. The institutional responsibilities are not only limited to providing quality technical education to students there by helping them for better employment or to make them entrepreneurs but also to ensure they imbibe human values. At KLS VDIT, we are committed to provide quality technical education to students and to serve the society through various initiatives. Through our interaction with public, the need for creating awareness about technology was felt. To felicitate general public in understanding technology in better manner, technology connectivity programs are being conducted.
Practise:
All India Radio Program on ‚ÄúTechnology for Common Man‚Äù, was arranged. Every day one faculty used to explain about a technology in Kannada. A total of 60 episodes were aired. To check the understanding of listeners, a question was asked every day. Prizes were given for one correct answer every day. Another program on All India Radio by Motivational speaker, Shri Gururaj Karajagi received very good response. The program was sponsored by the institute and was aimed to inculcate life values and ethics.
Computer Literacy Program has been conducted for high school students, Government Class IV Employees as well as for and senior citizens. Entrepreneurial development program is being conducted for high school and junior college students. The program is aimed to develop entrepreneurship mind-set amongst youngsters. This program is conducted in association with Government of Karnataka. Awareness has been created in different areas of life in nearby villages under¬†Unnat Bharat Abhiyan like digital transactions, electoral literacy drive, electrical energy saving, etc.
A technical Exhibition Centre has been established in campus with the help of industries. Students from nearby schools and colleges are encouraged to visit the centre and understand different technologies. To create a sense of belongingness and brotherhood among students, institute regularly conducts blood donation camp, and other socially relevant programs.
Students, parents and staff actively participated in ‚ÄúHar Ghar Thiranga‚Äù¬†Abhiyan. National anthem is played at morning 9.30 am on all working days in the institution.
Evidence of Success
A sense of belongingness and discipline is observed among students. Huge response is received for All India Radio Program. Good feedback has been received from students and others.
Problems Encountered and Resources required
Initial reluctance from public to learn technologies
Title 2:¬† Student value addition and industry connect
Objective
To enhance technical and employability skills among students and better industry connect for faculty.
The Context:
Over a period of time, it is observed that the syllabus prescribed by the university alone is not sufficient to update technical skills of students. Few courses need to be introduced, apart from university curriculum, to acquire better technical skills/ employability. Current industry practices need to be updated among students and faculty.
The practice:
Different online courses are being floated among students in different semesters of their study. During the academic year 2021-22 more than 250 students completed TCSiON career edge young professional certification. More than 500 students completed IIT Bombay Spoken Tutorial courses on Python 3.4.3, C and Cpp, Advanced Cpp, HTML, QCAD,¬†Blender, Scilab, eSim, OpenFOAM. Students have registered and completed TATA Ready Engineer program. Apart from nearby industries, internship is offered through AICTE Internshaala Portal, Microchip, Redhat Academy, Blue Prism University, CELONIS. Institute sponsored Faculty¬† for training at BOSCH Bangalore. Five faculty, one from each department, are trained for a period of one week in the month of April 2022. Students from Mechanical Engineering Department were sponsored for training at HAL Academy, Bangalore for 2 weeks starting from¬† 05/09/2022. Faculty are trained in different domains through Eduskills, Coursera, NPTEL, IIT Bombay Spoken Tutorial. One faculty- one consultancy initiative is taken.
Evidence of Success
The increase in i) number of publications by faculty in reputed journals ii) number pf patents published iii) funding received¬† and¬† improvement in number of placements are testimony.
Problems Encountered and Resources required`
Convincing the students to take up additional courses apart from university syllabus.

Umang-2025
Institutional Distinctiveness
Industry connect.
Research & Funding
Student Centric Activities.
Social Outreach Initiatives.
Industry Connect:
As a part of the Industry-Institute Interface, visits to industries are organized for students from time to time. Experts from Industries and reputed Institutes are invited for special talks. To commemorate Silver Jubilee Celebration of Visvesvaraya Technological University, KLS VDIT has organized 25 Technical Talks with Resource Persons from industry and institutes like IIT, NIT, etc. The Institute has established several Industry connections through active MoUs. Toyota Kirloskar Motors Bengaluru, Crevavi Technologies Pvt. Ltd., Germany, Advanced Electronics System, Bengaluru, HAEGL Technologies, Bengaluru, RTTC BSNL, Hyderabad, GTTC Siemens CoE, Dandeli, Enerzi Microwave Systems,¬† Belagavi, MPS Labs, Karnataka Rural Infrastructure Development Ltd. Bengaluru, Tech Fortune, Bengaluru, Sandbox¬† Startups, Hubballi, TATA Technologies Ltd, HAL Academy, Bengaluru, etc.
The institute has established Toyota Centre of Excellence. A Technical Exhibition Centre ‚ÄúJagruti‚Äù has been established in campus with the help of industries. Students from nearby Schools and Colleges are encouraged to visit the Centre and understand different technologies. Involvement of faculty in providing solutions to industry problems is ensured through ‚ÄúOne Faculty ‚Äì One Consultancy‚Äù initiative. Students are trained under Tata Ready Engineer program.
Research & Funding
Institute has implemented well defined Research & Development Policy. Funding received through New Age Incubation Network (NAIN), Vision Group on Science & Technology (VGST), Visvesvaraya Technological University, Karnatak State Council for Science & Technology, Karnataka Council of Technical Upgradation, etc. has motivated faculty and students to take up research work. Number of research papers published and a number of patents published by faculty is an indication of vibrant research culture.
Student Centric Activities.
Students are encouraged to participate in Curricular, Co-curricular and Extra Curricular activities in Intra and Inter institute levels. Mentoring of students is done by faculty. Faculty will guide the students based on their strengths and core competency. Students are undertaking Projects at first year. Field visits and Industrial visits are conducted regularly. Students prepare funding proposals and submit to Govt. agencies like KSCST, VTU, etc. Students take part in technical idea competitions and have won prizes. Sports facility available in the institute is being used by students under the guidance of Physical Director. Institute hosts various University level sports events. Students have bagged many prizes in sports at University level and represented University in inter University competitions. Cultural club takes care of activities for students. Music club facility is open to students. Students have participated and won prizes at State level events.
Social Outreach Initiatives:
The mission of institute is ‚Äúto inculcate culture of socially responsible citizenship‚Äù. The institute inculcates the culture of social responsibility among students through various activities conducted by NSS unit, Unnat Bharat Avhiyan, Department Associations, etc. Program aired on All India Radio regarding ‚ÄúTechnology for Common Man‚Äù and talk on ‚ÄúLife values and ethics‚Äù used to be shared with all students and parents through WhatsApp groups. Programs like Blood Donation Camps, Green Campus Initiatives, Awareness Programs to villagers, Electoral Literacy Drives, etc. have created a sense of responsible citizenship among students.

Research, Development and Innovation
Research, Development and Innovation
Objectives
Research Activities including Basic, Strategic, and Applied Research is undertaken for solving real-life problems.
Research Projects of Students at Undergraduate, Postgraduate, and Ph.D. Scholars have undertaken it as part of the curriculum or for additional enrichment.
Organizing and Conducting Motivational Talks, Seminars by Eminent Personalities for the students and faculty fraternity.
Preparation, Compilation, and Submission of Students and Faculty Research Project Proposals to a variety of Funding Agencies and to execute them well within deadlines.
Publications, Presentations, and Communication of the Research Outcomes to the external World.
Scholarly activities intended to expand knowledge boundaries by analysis, synthesis, and interpretation of ideas and information by making use of rigorous methodologies.
Preparation of¬† Theoretical on-paper designs, software simulations, prototype developments, experimentations, analyses, and documentation in the form of technical reports.
Research Facilities available in the department.
Click Here
Research Centre in Mechanical Engineering
The department is recognized as ‚ÄúResearch Center‚Äù in the year 2014-15 and offers Ph.D./ M.Sc.(Engg.) program by research, which is affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belgaum. The faculty members are actively involved in research activities. Major areas of research are thermal and fluids engineering, lean manufacturing, and Jet impingement.
Faculty members have published many research papers in their respective fields in international journals of high impact factors and have presented a good number of papers in national / international conferences and seminars.

Umang-2025
Research and Innovation in Department of CSE
Objectives
Research Activities including Basic, Strategic, and Applied Research is undertaken for solving real-life problems.
Research Projects of Students at Undergraduate and Ph.D. Scholars have undertaken it as part of the curriculum or for additional enrichment.
Organizing and Conducting Motivational Talks, Seminars by Eminent Personalities for the students and faculty fraternity.
Preparation, Compilation, and Submission of Students and Faculty Research Project Proposals to a variety of Funding Agencies and to execute them well within deadlines.
Publications, Presentations, and Communication of the Research Outcomes to the external World.
Scholarly activities intended to expand knowledge boundaries by analysis, synthesis, and interpretation of ideas and information by making use of rigorous methodologies.
Preparation of¬† Theoretical on-paper designs, software simulations, prototype developments, experimentations, analyses, and documentation in the form of technical reports.
Research Facilities available in the department.
Research Centre in Computer Science & Engineering
The department is recognized as ‚ÄúResearch Center‚Äù in the year 2023-24and offers Ph.D./ M.Sc.(Engg.) program by research, which is affiliated to Visvesvaraya Technological University, Belgaum. The faculty members are actively involved in research activities4
Faculty members have published many research papers in their respective fields in international journals of high impact factors and have presented a good number of papers in national / international conferences and seminars.

About VD-Hackathon
VD ‚Äì Hackathon is an exhilarating coding
challenge
where participants dive into a realm of creativity and problem ‚Äì solving!  Get ready  to  tackle intriguing problem statements  and  unleash your coding prowess
within the given time frame. Form a dream team   with  a   minimum of  2   and  a maximum of  4 members,   and embark on this exciting  coding  adventure  together.   This hackathon is not just a competition; it‚Äôs an opportunity for the students to showcase their skills, learn new technologies, and push the boundaries of innovation.

Adjunct Faculty
According to AICTE norm we should have three adjunct faculty members preferable industrial persons with more than 15 years of experience.
So for our department we have three adjunct faculty.
Shri Anant Kolhar,Vice President Mphasis HP Bangalore,
Shri Sripad K ,Head Capability Development ,Adobe systems India
Ravindra Kulkarni ,Program delivery Manager ,Persistent Sytems Ltd ,Pune
Role of adjunct faculty is to bridge the gap between Industry and academic institutions, Guiding our students regarding project proposals ,guidance to staff about project proposals , teaching methodology so on.
Shri Anant Kolhar, Vice President, Mphasis HP, Bangalore visited our department had interaction with faculty as well as students regarding project proposals.
How to choose and design Problem statement for project, Methodology to find solution, Importance of software engineering subject about waterfall model, agile development, incremental model in the industry ,cost ,risk management, project management . Basic Skills what we study in engineering are basic fundamental to build our future in corporate world.
